IF
    ActuallyInCombat()
    ActionListEmpty()
    See(NearestEnemyOf(Myself))
    HaveSpell(IDS)  // IDS (V1.0)
    Range(NearestEnemyOf(Myself),30)
    !GlobalTimerNotExpired("UNKNOWN_CAST","LOCALS")

    THEN
        RESPONSE #100
        Spell(NearestEnemyOf(Myself),IDS)  // Cast V1.0
        SetGlobalTimer("UNKNOWN_CAST","LOCALS",ONE_ROUND)
END
